function CreateCameras takes nothing returns nothing
	set gg_cam_Camera_001 = CreateCameraSetup()
	call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_Camera_001, CAMERA_FIELD_ZOFFSET, 0.0, 0.0)
	call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_Camera_001, CAMERA_FIELD_ROTATION, 90.0, 0.0)
	call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_Camera_001, CAMERA_FIELD_ANGLE_OF_ATTACK, 270.0, 0.0)
	call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_Camera_001, CAMERA_FIELD_TARGET_DISTANCE, 4660.0, 0.0)
	call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_Camera_001, CAMERA_FIELD_ROLL, 0.0, 0.0)
	call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_Camera_001, CAMERA_FIELD_FIELD_OF_VIEW, 40.0, 0.0)
	call CameraSetupSetField(gg_cam_Camera_001, CAMERA_FIELD_FARZ, 200.0, 0.0)
	call CameraSetupSetDestPosition(gg_cam_Camera_001,  - 1064.0,  - 280.0, 0.0)
endfunction

function InitTrig_Unbezeichneter_Ausl__ser_003 takes nothing returns nothing
	set gg_trg_Unbezeichneter_Ausl__ser_003 = CreateTrigger()
	call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Unbezeichneter_Ausl__ser_003, ref_function_Trig_Unbezeichneter_Ausl__ser_003_Actions)
endfunction

function InitCustomTriggers takes nothing returns nothing
	call InitTrig_Unbezeichneter_Ausl__ser_003()
endfunction

function InitGlobals takes nothing returns nothing
	call CreateTimer()
	call CreateGroup()
endfunction

function RunInitializationTriggers takes nothing returns nothing
	call ConditionalTriggerExecute(gg_trg_Unbezeichneter_Ausl__ser_003)
endfunction

function image_remove takes image this_42 returns nothing
	if this_42 != null then
		call DestroyImage(this_42)
	else
		call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exeption by destroying an image")
		call I2S(1 / 0)
	endif
endfunction

function hashtable_loadInt takes hashtable this_42, integer parentKey, integer childKey returns integer
	return LoadInteger(this_42, parentKey, childKey)
endfunction

function Table_loadInt takes integer this_42, integer parentKey returns integer
	return hashtable_loadInt(Table_ht, this_42, parentKey)
endfunction

function dispatch_Table_loadInt takes integer this_42, integer parentKey returns integer
	local integer loadInt_result
	if Table_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling Table.loadInt")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called Table.loadInt on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	set loadInt_result = Table_loadInt(this_42, parentKey)
	return loadInt_result
endfunction

function timer_getData takes timer this_42 returns integer
	return dispatch_Table_loadInt(TimerUtils_timerData, GetHandleId(this_42))
endfunction

function timer_pause takes timer this_42 returns nothing
	call PauseTimer(this_42)
endfunction

function hashtable_saveInt takes hashtable this_42, integer parentKey, integer childKey, integer value returns nothing
	call SaveInteger(this_42, parentKey, childKey, value)
endfunction

function Table_saveInt takes integer this_42, integer parentKey, integer value returns nothing
	call hashtable_saveInt(Table_ht, this_42, parentKey, value)
endfunction

function dispatch_Table_saveInt takes integer this_42, integer parentKey, integer value returns nothing
	if Table_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling Table.saveInt")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called Table.saveInt on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	call Table_saveInt(this_42, parentKey, value)
endfunction

function timer_setData takes timer this_42, integer data returns nothing
	call dispatch_Table_saveInt(TimerUtils_timerData, GetHandleId(this_42), data)
endfunction

function timer_release takes timer this_42 returns nothing
	if this_42 == null then
		call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Trying to release a null timer")
		call I2S(1 / 0)
		return
	endif
	if timer_getData(this_42) == TimerUtils_HELD then
		call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "ReleaseTimer: Double free!")
		call I2S(1 / 0)
		return
	endif
	call timer_setData(this_42, TimerUtils_HELD)
	call timer_pause(this_42)
	set TimerUtils_freeTimers[TimerUtils_freeTimersCount] = this_42
	set TimerUtils_freeTimersCount = TimerUtils_freeTimersCount + 1
endfunction

function AreaMarker_onDestroy takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	call image_remove(AreaMarker_img[this_42])
	if AreaMarker_t[this_42] != null then
		call timer_release(AreaMarker_t[this_42])
	endif
endfunction

function dealloc_AreaMarker takes integer obj returns nothing
	if AreaMarker_typeId[obj] == 0 then
		call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Double free: object of type AreaMarker")
		call I2S(1 / 0)
	else
		set AreaMarker_firstFree = AreaMarker_firstFree + 1
		set AreaMarker_typeId[obj] = 0
	endif
endfunction

function destroyAreaMarker takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	call AreaMarker_onDestroy(this_42)
	call dealloc_AreaMarker(this_42)
endfunction

		else

endfunction

function AreaMarker_destr takes nothing returns nothing
	call dispatch_AreaMarker_destroyAreaMarker(timer_getData(GetExpiredTimer()))
endfunction

function Action_onDestroy takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	if Event_first[Action_ev[this_42]] != this_42 then
		set Action_next[Action_prev[this_42]] = Action_next[this_42]
	else
		set Event_first[Action_ev[this_42]] = Action_next[this_42]
	endif
	if Event_last[Action_ev[this_42]] != this_42 then
		set Action_prev[Action_next[this_42]] = Action_prev[this_42]
	else
		set Event_last[Action_ev[this_42]] = Action_prev[this_42]
	endif
endfunction

function dealloc_Action takes integer obj returns nothing
	if Action_typeId[obj] == 0 then
		call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Double free: object of type Action")
		call I2S(1 / 0)
	else
		set Action_nextFree[Action_firstFree] = obj
		set Action_firstFree = Action_firstFree + 1
		set Action_typeId[obj] = 0
	endif
endfunction

function destroyAction takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	call Action_onDestroy(this_42)
	call dealloc_Action(this_42)
endfunction

function dispatch_Action_destroyAction takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	if Action_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling Action.destroyAction")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called Action.destroyAction on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	if Action_typeId[this_42] <= 671 then
		if Action_typeId[this_42] <= 667 then
			call destroyAction(this_42)
		else
			call destroyAction(this_42)
		endif
	elseif Action_typeId[this_42] <= 673 then
		call destroyAction(this_42)
	else
		call destroyAction(this_42)
	endif
endfunction

function unit_addAbility takes unit this_42, integer abil returns nothing
	call UnitAddAbility(this_42, abil)
endfunction

function unit_removeAbility takes unit this_42, integer abil returns nothing
	call UnitRemoveAbility(this_42, abil)
endfunction

function Unit_updateState takes integer this_42, integer amount_39, integer raw returns nothing
	local integer i
	local integer temp
	local integer statHelper
	local integer i_2
	local integer temp_2
	local integer i_3
	local integer temp_3
	call unit_removeAbility(Unit_u[this_42], raw + 45)
	set i = raw + 97
	set temp = raw + 97 + (Setup_maxBonSize - 1)
	loop
		exitwhen i > temp
		call unit_removeAbility(Unit_u[this_42], i)
		set i = i + 1
	endloop
	set statHelper = amount_39
	if statHelper >= 0 then
		set i_2 = raw + 97
		set temp_2 = raw + 97 + (Setup_maxBonSize - 1)
		loop
			exitwhen i_2 > temp_2
			if ModuloInteger(statHelper, 2) == 1 then
				call unit_addAbility(Unit_u[this_42], i_2)
			endif
			set statHelper = statHelper / 2
			if statHelper == 0 then
				return
			endif
			set i_2 = i_2 + 1
		endloop
	else
		set statHelper = statHelper + 1
		set i_3 = raw + 97
		set temp_3 = raw + 97 + (Setup_maxBonSize - 1)
		loop
			exitwhen i_3 > temp_3
			if ModuloInteger(statHelper, 2) == 0 then
				call unit_addAbility(Unit_u[this_42], i_3)
			endif
			set statHelper = statHelper / 2
			set i_3 = i_3 + 1
		endloop
		call unit_addAbility(Unit_u[this_42], raw + 45)
	endif
endfunction

function dispatch_Unit_updateState takes integer this_42, integer amount_39, integer raw returns nothing
	if Unit_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling Unit.updateState")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called Unit.updateState on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	if Unit_typeId[this_42] <= 693 then
		call Unit_updateState(this_42, amount_39, raw)
	else
		call Unit_updateState(this_42, amount_39, raw)
	endif
endfunction

function roundReal takes real value returns integer
	if value > 0. then
		return R2I(value + 0.5)
	else
		return R2I(value - 0.5)
	endif
endfunction

function Unit_updateLife takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	call dispatch_Unit_updateState(this_42, roundReal((Unit_life[this_42] + Unit_bonusLife[this_42]) * (1. + Unit_bonusLifePer[this_42] / 100.) - Unit_life[this_42]), Setup_lifeRaw)
endfunction

function getTimer takes nothing returns timer
	local timer receiver
	if TimerUtils_freeTimersCount > 0 then
		set TimerUtils_freeTimersCount = TimerUtils_freeTimersCount - 1
		call timer_setData(TimerUtils_freeTimers[TimerUtils_freeTimersCount], 0)
		set receiver = null
		return TimerUtils_freeTimers[TimerUtils_freeTimersCount]
	else
		set receiver = CreateTimer()
		call timer_setData(receiver, 0)
		set getTimertempReturn = receiver
		set receiver = null
		return getTimertempReturn
	endif
endfunction

function timer_start takes timer this_42, real time, code timerCallBack returns nothing
	call TimerStart(this_42, time, false, timerCallBack)
endfunction

function Bar_updateEx takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	local timer receiver = getTimer()
	local timer receiver_2
	call timer_setData(receiver, this_42)
	set receiver_2 = receiver
	call timer_start(receiver_2, 0.0, ref_function_Bar_callUpdateEx)
	set receiver = null
	set receiver_2 = null
endfunction

function dispatch_Bar_updateEx takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	if Bar_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling Bar.updateEx")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called Bar.updateEx on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	call Bar_updateEx(this_42)
endfunction

function alloc_LLEntry takes nothing returns integer
	local integer this_42
	if LLEntry_firstFree == 0 then
		set LLEntry_maxIndex = LLEntry_maxIndex + 1
		set this_42 = LLEntry_maxIndex
	else
		set LLEntry_firstFree = LLEntry_firstFree - 1
		set this_42 = LLEntry_nextFree[LLEntry_firstFree]
	endif
	set LLEntry_typeId[this_42] = 2
	return this_42
endfunction

function construct_LLEntry takes integer this_42, integer elem, integer prev, integer next returns nothing
	set LLEntry_elem[this_42] = elem
	set LLEntry_prev[this_42] = prev
	set LLEntry_next[this_42] = next
endfunction

function new_LLEntry takes integer elem, integer prev, integer next returns integer
	local integer this_42 = alloc_LLEntry()
	call construct_LLEntry(this_42, elem, prev, next)
	return this_42
endfunction

function LinkedList_add takes integer this_42, integer elem returns nothing
	local integer entry = new_LLEntry(elem, LLEntry_prev[LinkedList_dummy[this_42]], LinkedList_dummy[this_42])
	set LLEntry_next[LLEntry_prev[LinkedList_dummy[this_42]]] = entry
	set LLEntry_prev[LinkedList_dummy[this_42]] = entry
	set LinkedList_size[this_42] = LinkedList_size[this_42] + 1
endfunction

function dispatch_LinkedList_add takes integer this_42, integer elem returns nothing
	if LinkedList_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling LinkedList.add")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called LinkedList.add on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	call LinkedList_add(this_42, elem)
endfunction

function LLEntry_onDestroy takes integer this_42 returns nothing
endfunction

function dealloc_LLEntry takes integer obj returns nothing
	if LLEntry_typeId[obj] == 0 then
		call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Double free: object of type LLEntry")
		call I2S(1 / 0)
	else
		set LLEntry_nextFree[LLEntry_firstFree] = obj
		set LLEntry_firstFree = LLEntry_firstFree + 1
		set LLEntry_typeId[obj] = 0
	endif
endfunction

function destroyLLEntry takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	call LLEntry_onDestroy(this_42)
	call dealloc_LLEntry(this_42)
endfunction

function dispatch_LLEntry_destroyLLEntry takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	if LLEntry_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling LLEntry.destroyLLEntry")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called LLEntry.destroyLLEntry on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	call destroyLLEntry(this_42)
endfunction

function LinkedList_remove takes integer this_42, integer t returns nothing
	local integer r = LLEntry_next[LinkedList_dummy[this_42]]
	loop
		exitwhen  not (r != LinkedList_dummy[this_42])
		if LLEntry_elem[r] == t then
			set LLEntry_next[LLEntry_prev[r]] = LLEntry_next[r]
			set LLEntry_prev[LLEntry_next[r]] = LLEntry_prev[r]
			call dispatch_LLEntry_destroyLLEntry(r)
			set LinkedList_size[this_42] = LinkedList_size[this_42] - 1
			return
		endif
		set r = LLEntry_next[r]
	endloop
endfunction

function dispatch_LinkedList_remove takes integer this_42, integer t returns nothing
	if LinkedList_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling LinkedList.remove")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called LinkedList.remove on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif

function Unit_getMovespeed takes integer this_42, boolean withBonus returns real
	if withBonus then
		return (Unit_movespeed[this_42] + Unit_bonusMovespeed[this_42]) * (1. + Unit_bonusMovespeedPer[this_42] / 100.)
	else
		return Unit_movespeed[this_42]
	endif
endfunction

function dispatch_Unit_getMovespeed takes integer this_42, boolean withBonus returns real
	local real getMovespeed_result
	if Unit_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling Unit.getMovespeed")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called Unit.getMovespeed on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	if Unit_typeId[this_42] <= 693 then
		set getMovespeed_result = Unit_getMovespeed(this_42, withBonus)
	else
		set getMovespeed_result = Unit_getMovespeed(this_42, withBonus)
	endif
	return getMovespeed_result
endfunction

function Hero_updateMovespeed takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	call Unit_updateMovespeed(this_42)
	if dispatch_Unit_getMovespeed(this_42, true) > 522. then
		call dispatch_LinkedList_add(Hero_toMove, this_42)
	else
		call dispatch_LinkedList_remove(Hero_toMove, this_42)
	endif
endfunction

		endif
	endif

		if Bonus_typeId[this_42] <= 703 then
			if Bonus_typeId[this_42] <= 699 then
				if Bonus_typeId[this_42] <= 697 then

						call closure_impl_7(this_42)
					else
						call closure_impl_13(this_42)
					endif
				else

				endif

				call closure_impl_5(this_42)
			else
				call closure_impl_2(this_42)
			endif
		elseif Bonus_typeId[this_42] <= 709 then

					call closure_impl_8(this_42)
				else
					call closure_impl_10(this_42)

			else

		endif

function Buff_onDestroy takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	local integer tempIndex
	local integer tempTupleSelectionResult_1
	local integer temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1
	local integer temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2
	local integer tempIndex_2
	local integer tempTupleSelectionResult_2
	local integer temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2
	local integer temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2
	local unit temp
	local unit temp_2
	call dispatch_Action_destroyAction(Buff_action[this_42])
	call timer_release(Buff_t[this_42])
	call dispatch_LinkedList_remove(Unit_allBuffs[Buff_u[this_42]], this_42)
	if Buff_fxTimer[this_42] != null then
		call timer_release(Buff_fxTimer[this_42])
	endif
	set temp = Unit_u[Buff_u[this_42]]
	set tempIndex = this_42
	set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1 = Buff_btyp[tempIndex]
	set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2 = Buff_btyp_2[tempIndex]
	set tempTupleSelectionResult_1 = temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1
	call UnitRemoveAbility(temp, tempTupleSelectionResult_1)
	set temp_2 = Unit_u[Buff_u[this_42]]
	set tempIndex_2 = this_42
	set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2 = Buff_btyp[tempIndex_2]
	set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2 = Buff_btyp_2[tempIndex_2]
	set tempTupleSelectionResult_2 = temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2
	call UnitRemoveAbility(temp_2, tempTupleSelectionResult_2)
	if Buff_bon[this_42] != 0 then
		call dispatch_Bonus_destroyBonus(Buff_bon[this_42])
	endif
	if Buff_fx[this_42] != null then
		call DestroyEffect(Buff_fx[this_42])
	endif
	set temp = null
	set temp_2 = null
endfunction

function LinkedListModule_remove takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	set LinkedListModule_size = LinkedListModule_size - 1
	if this_42 != LinkedListModule_first then
		set LinkedListModule_next[LinkedListModule_prev[this_42]] = LinkedListModule_next[this_42]
	endif
	if this_42 != LinkedListModule_last then
		set LinkedListModule_prev[LinkedListModule_next[this_42]] = LinkedListModule_prev[this_42]
	endif
	if this_42 == LinkedListModule_last then
		set LinkedListModule_last = LinkedListModule_prev[this_42]
	endif
	if this_42 == LinkedListModule_first then
		set LinkedListModule_first = LinkedListModule_next[this_42]
	endif
endfunction

		set this_42 = SEntry_nextFree_2[SEntry_firstFree_2]
	endif
	return this_42
endfunction

	set SEntry_elem_2[this_42] = elem
	set SEntry_prev[this_42] = prev

	return this_42
endfunction

function Icon_isDisabled_get takes integer index1, integer index2 returns boolean
	local boolean returnVal
	if index2 < 0 or index2 >= 12 then
		call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Index out of Bounds")
		call I2S(1 / 0)
	elseif index2 <= 5 then
		if index2 <= 2 then
			if index2 <= 1 then
				if index2 <= 0 then
					set returnVal = Icon_isDisabled_0[index1]
				else
					set returnVal = Icon_isDisabled_1[index1]
				endif
			else
				set returnVal = Icon_isDisabled_2[index1]
			endif
		elseif index2 <= 4 then
			if index2 <= 3 then
				set returnVal = Icon_isDisabled_3[index1]
			else
				set returnVal = Icon_isDisabled_4[index1]
			endif
		else
			set returnVal = Icon_isDisabled_5[index1]
		endif
	elseif index2 <= 8 then
		if index2 <= 7 then
			if index2 <= 6 then
				set returnVal = Icon_isDisabled_6[index1]
			else
				set returnVal = Icon_isDisabled_7[index1]
			endif
		else
			set returnVal = Icon_isDisabled_8[index1]
		endif
	elseif index2 <= 10 then
		if index2 <= 9 then
			set returnVal = Icon_isDisabled_9[index1]
		else
			set returnVal = Icon_isDisabled_10[index1]
		endif
	else
		set returnVal = Icon_isDisabled_11[index1]
	endif
	return returnVal
endfunction

function Icon_showDirect takes integer this_42, player p returns nothing
	local destructable d_2 = Icon_structs_get(this_42, player_getId(p))
	local integer id
	local integer tempIndex
	local integer tempTupleSelectionResult_2
	local integer temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1
	local integer temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2
	local integer tempIndex_2
	local integer tempTupleSelectionResult_1
	local integer temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2
	local integer temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2
	local integer tempIndex_3
	local real tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_3
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_3
	local integer tempIndex_4
	local real tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_4
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_4
	local integer temp
	local real temp_2
	local integer temp_3
	local integer temp_4
	if d_2 == null then
		set id = Icon_dummyIcon
		if GetLocalPlayer() == p then
			if Icon_isDisabled_get(this_42, player_getId(p)) then
				set tempIndex = this_42
				set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1 = Icon_typ[tempIndex]
				set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2 = Icon_typ_2[tempIndex]
				set tempTupleSelectionResult_2 = temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2
				set id = tempTupleSelectionResult_2
				call print("is Disabled")
			else
				set tempIndex_2 = this_42
				set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2 = Icon_typ[tempIndex_2]
				set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2 = Icon_typ_2[tempIndex_2]
				set tempTupleSelectionResult_1 = temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2
				set id = tempTupleSelectionResult_1
			endif
		endif
		set temp_3 = this_42
		set temp_4 = player_getId(p)
		set temp = id
		set tempIndex_3 = this_42
		set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_3 = Icon_realPos[tempIndex_3]
		set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_3 = Icon_realPos_2[tempIndex_3]
		set tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2 = temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_3
		set temp_2 = tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2
		set tempIndex_4 = this_42
		set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_4 = Icon_realPos[tempIndex_4]
		set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_4 = Icon_realPos_2[tempIndex_4]
		set tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2 = temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_4
		call Icon_structs_set(temp_3, temp_4, CreateDestructable(temp, temp_2, tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2, 0., Icon_scale[this_42] * 1., 1))
	endif
	set d_2 = null
endfunction

function image_show takes image this_42, player p returns nothing
	if GetLocalPlayer() == p then
		call SetImageRenderAlways(this_42, true)
	endif
endfunction

function ImageEx_showDirect takes integer this_42, player p returns nothing
	call image_show(ImageEx_content[this_42], p)
endfunction

function color_withAlpha takes integer this_red, integer this_green, integer this_blue, integer a returns integer
	set color_withAlpha_return_red = this_red
	set color_withAlpha_return_green = this_green
	set color_withAlpha_return_blue = this_blue
	set color_withAlpha_return_alpha = a
	return color_withAlpha_return_red
endfunction

function unit_setVertexColor takes unit this_42, integer col_red, integer col_green, integer col_blue, integer col_alpha returns nothing
	call SetUnitVertexColor(this_42, col_red, col_green, col_blue, col_alpha)
endfunction

function Model_showDirect takes integer this_42, player p returns nothing
	local unit temp = Model_u[this_42]
	local integer tempIndex = this_42
	call unit_setVertexColor(temp, color_withAlpha(Model_col[tempIndex], Model_col_2[tempIndex], Model_col_3[tempIndex], 255), color_withAlpha_return_green, color_withAlpha_return_blue, color_withAlpha_return_alpha)
	set temp = null
endfunction

function char takes string s returns integer
	local integer a
	if "\\" == s then
		return 92
	endif
	set a = Char_s2c[StringHash(s) / 2033480 + 1002]
	if s != Char_c2s[a] then
		return a + 32
	endif
	return a
endfunction

function alloc_ImageListEntry takes nothing returns integer
	local integer this_42
	if ImageListEntry_firstFree == 0 then
		set ImageListEntry_maxIndex = ImageListEntry_maxIndex + 1
		set this_42 = ImageListEntry_maxIndex
	else
		set ImageListEntry_firstFree = ImageListEntry_firstFree - 1
		set this_42 = ImageListEntry_nextFree[ImageListEntry_firstFree]
	endif
	set ImageListEntry_typeId[this_42] = 777
	return this_42
endfunction

function construct_ImageListEntry takes integer this_42, image img, integer prev returns nothing
	set ImageListEntry_img[this_42] = img
	set ImageListEntry_prev[this_42] = prev
endfunction

function new_ImageListEntry takes image img, integer prev returns integer
	local integer this_42 = alloc_ImageListEntry()
	call construct_ImageListEntry(this_42, img, prev)
	return this_42
endfunction

function ImageList_add takes integer this_42, image i returns nothing
	set ImageList_last[this_42] = new_ImageListEntry(i, ImageList_last[this_42])
endfunction

function dispatch_ImageList_add takes integer this_42, image i returns nothing
	if ImageList_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling ImageList.add")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called ImageList.add on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	call ImageList_add(this_42, i)
endfunction

function TextSplat_updateDimY takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	local integer tempIndex = this_42
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1 = TextSplat_cursor[tempIndex]
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2 = TextSplat_cursor_2[tempIndex]
	local real tempTupleSelectionResult_2 = temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2
	local real temp = tempTupleSelectionResult_2
	local integer tempIndex_2 = this_42
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2 = TextSplat_dimensions[tempIndex_2]
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2 = TextSplat_dimensions_2[tempIndex_2]
	local real tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2 = temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2
	local integer tempIndex_3
	local integer tempIndex_4
	local real tempTupleSelectionResult_2_3
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_3
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_3
	if temp < tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2 then
		set tempIndex_3 = this_42
		set tempIndex_4 = this_42
		set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_3 = TextSplat_cursor[tempIndex_4]
		set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_3 = TextSplat_cursor_2[tempIndex_4]
		set tempTupleSelectionResult_2_3 = temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_3
		set TextSplat_dimensions_2[tempIndex_3] = tempTupleSelectionResult_2_3
	endif
endfunction

function dispatch_TextSplat_updateDimY takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	if TextSplat_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling TextSplat.updateDimY")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called TextSplat.updateDimY on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	call TextSplat_updateDimY(this_42)
endfunction

function getFontHeight takes nothing returns integer
	return FontArial_FONT_HEIGHT
endfunction

function getFontResolution takes nothing returns integer
	return FontArial_FONT_RESOLUTION
endfunction

function TextSplat_newline takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	local integer tempIndex = this_42
	local integer tempIndex_2 = this_42
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1 = TextSplat_pos[tempIndex_2]
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2 = TextSplat_pos_2[tempIndex_2]
	local real tempTupleSelectionResult_1 = temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1
	local integer tempIndex_3
	local integer tempIndex_4
	local real tempTupleSelectionResult_2
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2
	local integer temp
	set TextSplat_cursor[tempIndex] = tempTupleSelectionResult_1
	set tempIndex_3 = this_42
	set temp = tempIndex_3
	set tempIndex_4 = this_42
	set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2 = TextSplat_cursor[tempIndex_4]
	set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2 = TextSplat_cursor_2[tempIndex_4]
	set tempTupleSelectionResult_2 = temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2
	set TextSplat_cursor_2[temp] = tempTupleSelectionResult_2 - TextSplat_fontSize[this_42] * getFontHeight() / getFontResolution()
	call dispatch_TextSplat_updateDimY(this_42)
endfunction

function dispatch_TextSplat_newline takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	if TextSplat_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling TextSplat.newline")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called TextSplat.newline on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	call TextSplat_newline(this_42)
endfunction

function TextSplat_updateDimX takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	local integer tempIndex = this_42
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1 = TextSplat_cursor[tempIndex]
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2 = TextSplat_cursor_2[tempIndex]
	local real tempTupleSelectionResult_1 = temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1
	local real temp = tempTupleSelectionResult_1
	local integer tempIndex_2 = this_42
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2 = TextSplat_dimensions[tempIndex_2]
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2 = TextSplat_dimensions_2[tempIndex_2]
	local real tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2 = temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2
	local integer tempIndex_3
	local integer tempIndex_4
	local real tempTupleSelectionResult_1_3
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_3
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_3
	if temp > tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2 then
		set tempIndex_3 = this_42
		set tempIndex_4 = this_42
		set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_3 = TextSplat_cursor[tempIndex_4]
		set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_3 = TextSplat_cursor_2[tempIndex_4]
		set tempTupleSelectionResult_1_3 = temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_3
		set TextSplat_dimensions[tempIndex_3] = tempTupleSelectionResult_1_3
	endif
endfunction

function dispatch_TextSplat_updateDimX takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	if TextSplat_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling TextSplat.updateDimX")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called TextSplat.updateDimX on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	call TextSplat_updateDimX(this_42)
endfunction

function char_toInt takes integer this_c returns integer
	return this_c
endfunction

function getFontPath takes integer c_c returns string
	return FontArial_paths[char_toInt(c_c)]
endfunction

function getFontWidth takes integer c_c returns integer
	return FontArial_widths[char_toInt(c_c)]
endfunction

function image_setColor takes image this_42, integer col_red, integer col_green, integer col_blue, integer col_alpha returns nothing

endfunction

function image_show_2 takes image this_42 returns nothing
	call SetImageRenderAlways(this_42, true)
endfunction

function string_charAt takes string this_42, integer index returns string
	return SubString(this_42, index, index + 1)
endfunction

function string_length takes string this_42 returns integer
	return StringLength(this_42)
endfunction

function TextSplat_append takes integer this_42, string text, integer col_red, integer col_green, integer col_blue, integer col_alpha, player p returns nothing
	local integer c_c
	local real charWidth
	local integer n
	local integer temp
	local image img
	local image receiver
	local integer tempIndex
	local real tempTupleSelectionResult_1
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2
	local integer tempIndex_2
	local real tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2
	local integer tempIndex_3
	local real tempTupleSelectionResult_2
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_3
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_3
	local integer tempIndex_4
	local integer tempIndex_5
	local real tempTupleSelectionResult_1_3
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_4
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_4
	local string temp_2
	local real temp_3
	local real temp_4
	local real temp_5
	local integer temp_6
	if GetLocalPlayer() == p then
		set n = 0
		set temp = string_length(text) - 1
		loop
			exitwhen n > temp
			set c_c = char(string_charAt(text, n))
			set charWidth = TextSplat_fontSize[this_42] * getFontWidth(c_c) / getFontResolution()
			set tempIndex = this_42
			set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1 = TextSplat_cursor[tempIndex]
			set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2 = TextSplat_cursor_2[tempIndex]
			set tempTupleSelectionResult_1 = temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1
			if tempTupleSelectionResult_1 + charWidth > TextSplat_maxWidth[this_42] then
				call dispatch_TextSplat_newline(this_42)
			endif
			if c_c != 32 then
				set temp_2 = getFontPath(c_c)
				set temp_3 = TextSplat_fontSize[this_42]
				set temp_4 = TextSplat_fontSize[this_42]
				set tempIndex_2 = this_42
				set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2 = TextSplat_cursor[tempIndex_2]
				set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2 = TextSplat_cursor_2[tempIndex_2]
				set tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2 = temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2
				set temp_5 = tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2
				set tempIndex_3 = this_42
				set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_3 = TextSplat_cursor[tempIndex_3]
				set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_3 = TextSplat_cursor_2[tempIndex_3]
				set tempTupleSelectionResult_2 = temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_3
				set receiver = CreateImage(temp_2, temp_3, temp_4, 0., temp_5, tempTupleSelectionResult_2, 0., 0., 0., 0., TextSplat_layer[this_42] + 1)
				call image_show_2(receiver)
				set img = receiver
				if col_alpha != TextSplat_DISABLE_COLOR_ALPHA then
					call image_setColor(img, col_red, col_green, col_blue, col_alpha)
				endif
				call dispatch_ImageList_add(TextSplat_images[this_42], img)
			endif
			set tempIndex_4 = this_42
			set temp_6 = tempIndex_4
			set tempIndex_5 = this_42
			set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_4 = TextSplat_cursor[tempIndex_5]
			set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_4 = TextSplat_cursor_2[tempIndex_5]
			set tempTupleSelectionResult_1_3 = temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_4
			set TextSplat_cursor[temp_6] = tempTupleSelectionResult_1_3 + charWidth
			call dispatch_TextSplat_updateDimX(this_42)
			set n = n + 1
		endloop
	endif
	set img = null
	set receiver = null
endfunction

function dispatch_TextSplat_append takes integer this_42, string text, integer col_red, integer col_green, integer col_blue, integer col_alpha, player p returns nothing
	if TextSplat_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling TextSplat.append")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called TextSplat.append on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	call TextSplat_append(this_42, text, col_red, col_green, col_blue, col_alpha, p)
endfunction

function ImageListEntry_onDestroy takes integer this_42 returns nothing
endfunction

function dealloc_ImageListEntry takes integer obj returns nothing
	if ImageListEntry_typeId[obj] == 0 then
		call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Double free: object of type ImageListEntry")
		call I2S(1 / 0)
	else
		set ImageListEntry_nextFree[ImageListEntry_firstFree] = obj
		set ImageListEntry_firstFree = ImageListEntry_firstFree + 1
		set ImageListEntry_typeId[obj] = 0
	endif
endfunction

	call ImageListEntry_onDestroy(this_42)
	call dealloc_ImageListEntry(this_42)
endfunction

			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called ImageListEntry.destroyImageListEntry on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	call destroyImageListEntry(this_42)
endfunction

function ImageList_eraseAll takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	local integer e = ImageList_last[this_42]
	loop
		exitwhen  not (e != 0)
		call image_remove(ImageListEntry_img[e])
		call dispatch_ImageListEntry_destroyImageListEntry(e)
		set e = ImageListEntry_prev[e]
	endloop
	set ImageList_last[this_42] = 0
endfunction

function dispatch_ImageList_eraseAll takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	if ImageList_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling ImageList.eraseAll")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called ImageList.eraseAll on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	call ImageList_eraseAll(this_42)
endfunction

function TextSplat_clear takes integer this_42, player p returns nothing
	local integer tempIndex
	local integer tempIndex_2
	local real tempTupleSelectionResult_1
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2
	local integer tempIndex_3
	local real tempTupleSelectionResult_2
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2
	local integer tempIndex_4
	local integer tempIndex_5
	local integer temp
	local integer temp_2
	if GetLocalPlayer() == p then
		call dispatch_ImageList_eraseAll(TextSplat_images[this_42])
		set tempIndex = this_42
		set temp = tempIndex
		set tempIndex_2 = this_42
		set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1 = TextSplat_pos[tempIndex_2]
		set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2 = TextSplat_pos_2[tempIndex_2]
		set tempTupleSelectionResult_1 = temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1
		set TextSplat_cursor[temp] = tempTupleSelectionResult_1
		set temp_2 = tempIndex
		set tempIndex_3 = this_42
		set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2 = TextSplat_pos[tempIndex_3]
		set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2 = TextSplat_pos_2[tempIndex_3]
		set tempTupleSelectionResult_2 = temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2
		set TextSplat_cursor_2[temp_2] = tempTupleSelectionResult_2 - TextSplat_fontSize[this_42]
		set tempIndex_4 = this_42
		set tempIndex_5 = this_42
		set TextSplat_dimensions[tempIndex_4] = TextSplat_pos[tempIndex_5]
		set TextSplat_dimensions_2[tempIndex_4] = TextSplat_pos_2[tempIndex_5]
	endif
endfunction

function dispatch_TextSplat_clear takes integer this_42, player p returns nothing
	if TextSplat_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling TextSplat.clear")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called TextSplat.clear on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	call TextSplat_clear(this_42, p)
endfunction

function TextBox_showDirect takes integer this_42, player p returns nothing
	local integer tempIndex
	local integer temp
	local string temp_2
	call dispatch_TextSplat_clear(TextBox_splat[this_42], p)
	set temp = TextBox_splat[this_42]
	set temp_2 = TextBox_content[this_42]
	set tempIndex = this_42
	call dispatch_TextSplat_append(temp, temp_2, color_withAlpha(TextBox_col[tempIndex], TextBox_col_2[tempIndex], TextBox_col_3[tempIndex], 255), color_withAlpha_return_green, color_withAlpha_return_blue, color_withAlpha_return_alpha, p)
endfunction

	return ImageIterator_nexttempReturn

	set next_result = null

function alloc_ImageIterator takes nothing returns integer
	local integer this_42
	if ImageIterator_firstFree == 0 then
		set ImageIterator_maxIndex = ImageIterator_maxIndex + 1
		set this_42 = ImageIterator_maxIndex
	else
		set ImageIterator_firstFree = ImageIterator_firstFree - 1
		set this_42 = ImageIterator_nextFree[ImageIterator_firstFree]
	endif
	set ImageIterator_typeId[this_42] = 796
	return this_42
endfunction

	set ImageIterator_pos[this_42] = start
endfunction

	local integer this_42 = alloc_ImageIterator()
	call construct_ImageIterator(this_42, start)
	return this_42
endfunction

function alloc_LLIterator takes nothing returns integer
	local integer this_42
	if LLIterator_firstFree == 0 then
		set LLIterator_maxIndex = LLIterator_maxIndex + 1
		set this_42 = LLIterator_maxIndex
	else
		set LLIterator_firstFree = LLIterator_firstFree - 1
		set this_42 = LLIterator_nextFree[LLIterator_firstFree]
	endif
	set LLIterator_typeId[this_42] = 3
	return this_42
endfunction

function construct_LLIterator takes integer this_42, integer dummy returns nothing
	set LLIterator_dummy[this_42] = dummy
	set LLIterator_current[this_42] = dummy
endfunction

	local integer this_42 = alloc_LLIterator()
	call construct_LLIterator(this_42, dummy)
	return this_42
endfunction

function cyc_cyc_dispatch_Widget_showDirect takes integer funcChoice, integer funcChoice_2, integer this_42, player p returns nothing
	local integer wurst__iterator1
	local image img
	local integer wurst__iterator2
	local integer w_2
	if funcChoice == 0 then
		if funcChoice_2 == 0 then
			if Widget_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
				if this_42 == 0 then
					call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling Widget.showDirect")
					call I2S(1 / 0)
				else
					call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called Widget.showDirect on invalid object.")
					call I2S(1 / 0)
				endif
			endif
			if Widget_typeId[this_42] <= 797 then
				if Widget_typeId[this_42] <= 792 then
					if Widget_typeId[this_42] <= 784 then
						call cyc_cyc_dispatch_Widget_showDirect(0, 2, this_42, p)
					else
						call TextBox_showDirect(this_42, p)
					endif
				elseif Widget_typeId[this_42] <= 793 then
					call ImageEx_showDirect(this_42, p)
				else
					call cyc_cyc_dispatch_Widget_showDirect(1, this_42, 0, p)
				endif
			elseif Widget_typeId[this_42] <= 805 then
				if Widget_typeId[this_42] <= 801 then
					call Model_showDirect(this_42, p)
				else
					call Icon_showDirect(this_42, p)
				endif
			else
				call cyc_cyc_dispatch_Widget_showDirect(0, 1, this_42, p)
			endif
		elseif funcChoice_2 == 1 then
			call dispatch_TextSplat_append_2(Button_splat[this_42], Button_name[this_42], p)
			call cyc_cyc_dispatch_Widget_showDirect(0, 2, this_42, p)
		elseif funcChoice_2 == 2 then
			call cyc_cyc_dispatch_Widget_showDirect(0, 0, Observable_content[this_42], p)
		endif
	elseif funcChoice == 1 then
		if GetLocalPlayer() == p then
			set wurst__iterator1 = dispatch_ImageList_iterator(Pane_list[funcChoice_2])
			loop
				exitwhen  not dispatch_ImageIterator_hasNext(wurst__iterator1)
				set img = dispatch_ImageIterator_next(wurst__iterator1)
				call image_show_2(img)
			endloop
			call dispatch_ImageIterator_close(wurst__iterator1)
			set wurst__iterator2 = dispatch_LinkedList_iterator(Pane_content[funcChoice_2])
			loop
				exitwhen  not dispatch_LLIterator_hasNext(wurst__iterator2)
				set w_2 = dispatch_LLIterator_next(wurst__iterator2)
				call cyc_cyc_dispatch_Widget_showDirect(0, 0, w_2, p)
			endloop
			call dispatch_LLIterator_close(wurst__iterator2)
		endif
	endif
	set img = null
endfunction

		if Action_typeId[this_42] <= 671 then
			call closure_impl_21(this_42, d_2)
		else

	else
		call closure_impl_22(this_42, d_2)
	endif
endfunction

function Event_stop takes integer this_42, integer d_2 returns boolean
	return false
endfunction

function OnDamageEvent_stop takes integer this_42, integer data returns boolean
	return OnDamageData_stop[data]
endfunction

function SpellEvent_stop takes integer this_42, integer data returns boolean
	return  not SpellData_spellSuccess[data]
endfunction

function dispatch_Event_stop takes integer this_42, integer d_2 returns boolean
	local boolean stop_result
	if Event_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling Event.stop")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called Event.stop on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	if Event_typeId[this_42] <= 765 then
		if Event_typeId[this_42] <= 763 then
			if Event_typeId[this_42] <= 666 then
				set stop_result = Event_stop(this_42, d_2)
			else
				set stop_result = Event_stop(this_42, d_2)
			endif
		else
			set stop_result = OnDamageEvent_stop(this_42, d_2)
		endif
	elseif Event_typeId[this_42] <= 768 then
		if Event_typeId[this_42] <= 767 then
			set stop_result = SpellEvent_stop(this_42, d_2)
		else
			set stop_result = Event_stop(this_42, d_2)
		endif
	else
		set stop_result = Event_stop(this_42, d_2)
	endif
	return stop_result
endfunction

function Event_callActions takes integer this_42, integer d_2 returns nothing
	local integer buffer = Event_first[this_42]
	if Event_checkData[this_42] then
		loop
			exitwhen  not (buffer != 0)
			if dispatch_Event_stop(this_42, d_2) then
				return
			endif
			call dispatch_Action_fire(buffer, d_2)
			set buffer = Action_next[buffer]
		endloop
	else
		loop
			exitwhen  not (buffer != 0)
			call dispatch_Action_fire(buffer, d_2)
			set buffer = Action_next[buffer]
		endloop
	endif
endfunction

function UnitEvent_fire takes integer this_42, integer whichUnit returns nothing
	call Event_callActions(this_42, whichUnit)
endfunction

	call ForGroup(this_42, ref_function_GroupAddGroupEnum_2)
	return bj_groupAddGroupDest
endfunction

	call GroupRemoveUnit(this_42, u_2)
	set group_nexttempReturn = u_2
	set u_2 = null
	return group_nexttempReturn
endfunction

function real_squared takes real this_42 returns real
	return this_42 * this_42
endfunction

function vec2_distToVec takes real this_x, real this_y, real v_x, real v_y returns real
	return SquareRoot(real_squared(v_x - this_x) + real_squared(v_y - this_y))
endfunction

function Aura_check takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	local group wurst__iterator0 = group_iterator(Aura_g[this_42])
	local unit gu
	local integer obj
	local group tempGroup
	local unit gu_2
	local integer obj_2
	loop
		exitwhen  not group_hasNext(wurst__iterator0)
		set gu = group_next(wurst__iterator0)
		set obj = unit_getUserData(gu)
		if obj != 0 and vec2_distToVec(unit_getPos(gu), unit_getPos_return_y, unit_getPos(Unit_u[Aura_u[this_42]]), unit_getPos_return_y) > Aura_radius[this_42] then
			call dispatch_UnitEvent_fire(Aura_leave[this_42], obj)
			call GroupRemoveUnit(Aura_g[this_42], gu)
		endif
	endloop
	call group_close(wurst__iterator0)
	set tempGroup = CreateGroup()
	call MoveRectTo(Aura_r[this_42], unit_getX(Unit_u[Aura_u[this_42]]), unit_getY(Unit_u[Aura_u[this_42]]))
	call GroupEnumUnitsInRect(tempGroup, Aura_r[this_42], Aura_filter[this_42])
	loop
		exitwhen  not group_hasNext(tempGroup)
		set gu_2 = group_next(tempGroup)
		set obj_2 = unit_getUserData(gu_2)
		if obj_2 != 0 and vec2_distToVec(unit_getPos(gu_2), unit_getPos_return_y, unit_getPos(Unit_u[Aura_u[this_42]]), unit_getPos_return_y) <= Aura_radius[this_42] and ( not IsUnitInGroup(gu_2, Aura_g[this_42])) then
			call dispatch_UnitEvent_fire(Aura_enter[this_42], obj_2)
			call GroupAddUnit(Aura_g[this_42], gu_2)
		endif
	endloop
	call DestroyGroup(tempGroup)
	set wurst__iterator0 = null
	set gu = null
	set tempGroup = null
	set gu_2 = null
endfunction

function dispatch_Aura_check takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	if Aura_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling Aura.check")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called Aura.check on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif

endfunction

function unit_getState takes unit this_42, unitstate state returns real
	return GetUnitState(this_42, state)

function unit_getHP takes unit this_42 returns real
	return unit_getState(this_42, UNIT_STATE_LIFE)

function Bar_update takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	local real hp = unit_getHP(Unit_u[Bar_owner[this_42]])
	local real maxHp = GetUnitState(Unit_u[Bar_owner[this_42]], UNIT_STATE_MAX_LIFE)
	local real per = hp / maxHp
	local integer barsGot = roundReal(per * HeroBar_realBarCount) * 2
	local integer shieldBars = roundReal(ShieldList_shieldSum[Unit_shieldList[Bar_owner[this_42]]] / maxHp * HeroBar_realBarCount) * 2
	local integer barsLeft = HeroBar_fakeBarCount - barsGot - shieldBars
	local string hpGot
	local string shield
	local integer manaBarsGot
	local integer manaBarsLeft
	local string manaGot
	local string manaDead
	local string final
	set barsGot = barsGot + barsGot / (Bar_markerDistance[this_42] + 2) * 12
	set hpGot = SubString(Bar_hpFull[this_42], 0, barsGot)
	set shield = SubString(HeroBar_bar, 0, shieldBars)
	set manaBarsGot = roundReal(GetUnitState(Unit_u[Bar_owner[this_42]], UNIT_STATE_MANA) / GetUnitState(Unit_u[Bar_owner[this_42]], UNIT_STATE_MAX_MANA) * HeroBar_realBarCount) * 2
	set manaBarsLeft = HeroBar_fakeBarCount - manaBarsGot
	set manaGot = SubString(HeroBar_bar, 0, manaBarsGot)
	set manaDead = SubString(HeroBar_bar, 0, manaBarsLeft)
	if barsLeft <= 0 then
		set final = hpGot + HeroBar_shieldColor + shield + HeroBar_endColor + "|n" + HeroBar_mpColor + manaGot + HeroBar_endColor + HeroBar_mpColorDead + manaDead + HeroBar_endColor
	else
		set final = hpGot + HeroBar_shieldColor + shield + HeroBar_endColor + HeroBar_hpColorDead + SubString(HeroBar_bar, 0, barsLeft) + HeroBar_endColor + "|n" + HeroBar_mpColor + manaGot + HeroBar_endColor + HeroBar_mpColorDead + manaDead + HeroBar_endColor
	endif
	call SetTextTagText(Bar_tt[this_42], final, 0.01)
endfunction

function dispatch_Bar_update takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	if Bar_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling Bar.update")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called Bar.update on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	call Bar_update(this_42)
endfunction

function Bar_updateExDirect takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	local integer i
	local integer temp
	local integer charCount
	set Bar_markerDistance[this_42] = (HeroBar_seperateAt * HeroBar_realBarCount / R2I(GetUnitState(Unit_u[Bar_owner[this_42]], UNIT_STATE_MAX_LIFE)) - 1) * 2
	set Bar_hpFull[this_42] = ""
	set i = 1
	set temp = HeroBar_fakeBarCount / (Bar_markerDistance[this_42] + 2)
	loop
		exitwhen i > temp
		set Bar_hpFull[this_42] = Bar_hpFull[this_42] + SubString(HeroBar_bar, 0, Bar_markerDistance[this_42])
		set Bar_hpFull[this_42] = Bar_hpFull[this_42] + HeroBar_marker
		set i = i + 1
	endloop
	set charCount = HeroBar_fakeBarCount / (Bar_markerDistance[this_42] + 2) * (Bar_markerDistance[this_42] + 2)
	set Bar_hpFull[this_42] = Bar_hpFull[this_42] + SubString(HeroBar_bar, 0, HeroBar_fakeBarCount - charCount)
	call dispatch_Bar_update(this_42)
endfunction

function dispatch_Bar_updateExDirect takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	if Bar_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling Bar.updateExDirect")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called Bar.updateExDirect on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	call Bar_updateExDirect(this_42)
endfunction

function Bar_callUpdateEx takes nothing returns nothing
	local timer t = GetExpiredTimer()
	call dispatch_Bar_updateExDirect(timer_getData(t))
	call timer_release(t)
	set t = null
	set t = null
endfunction

	set Hero_getBarPos_return_y = unit_getY(Unit_u[this_42])
	set Hero_getBarPos_return_z = GetUnitFlyHeight(Unit_u[this_42]) + Unit_height[this_42]
	return Hero_getBarPos_return_x
endfunction

function dispatch_Hero_getBarPos takes integer this_42 returns real
	local real getBarPos_result_x
	local real getBarPos_result_y
	local real getBarPos_result_z
	local real temp_getBarPos_result_x
	local real temp_getBarPos_result_y
	local real temp_getBarPos_result_z
	if Unit_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling Hero.getBarPos")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called Hero.getBarPos on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	set temp_getBarPos_result_x = Hero_getBarPos(this_42)
	set temp_getBarPos_result_y = Hero_getBarPos_return_y
	set temp_getBarPos_result_z = Hero_getBarPos_return_z
	set getBarPos_result_x = temp_getBarPos_result_x
	set getBarPos_result_y = temp_getBarPos_result_y
	set getBarPos_result_z = temp_getBarPos_result_z
	set dispatch_Hero_getBarPos_return_x = getBarPos_result_x
	set dispatch_Hero_getBarPos_return_y = getBarPos_result_y
	set dispatch_Hero_getBarPos_return_z = getBarPos_result_z
	return dispatch_Hero_getBarPos_return_x
endfunction

			call texttag_setPos(Bar_tt[b], dispatch_Hero_getBarPos(Bar_owner[b]), dispatch_Hero_getBarPos_return_y, dispatch_Hero_getBarPos_return_z)

	endloop

function Bar_updateVision_2 takes nothing returns nothing
	local integer b = LinkedListModule_first_2
	loop
		exitwhen  not (b != 0)
		if Bar_check[b] then
			if IsVisibleToPlayer(unit_getX(Unit_u[Bar_owner[b]]), unit_getY(Unit_u[Bar_owner[b]]), GetLocalPlayer()) then
				set Bar_isVisible[b] = true
				call texttag_setVisibility(Bar_tt[b], true)
			else
				set Bar_isVisible[b] = false
				call texttag_setVisibility(Bar_tt[b], false)
			endif
			call dispatch_Bar_update(b)
			set b = LinkedListModule_next_2[b]
		endif
	endloop
endfunction

function unit_addEffect takes unit this_42, string fx, string attachment returns effect
	return AddSpecialEffectTarget(fx, this_42, attachment)
endfunction

function Buff_createEffect takes nothing returns nothing
	local timer t = GetExpiredTimer()
	local integer b = timer_getData(t)
	if Buff_fxCounter[b] > 0 then
		call DestroyEffect(unit_addEffect(Unit_u[Buff_u[b]], Buff_fxType[b], Buff_attachment[b]))
		set Buff_fxCounter[b] = Buff_fxCounter[b] - 1
	else
		call timer_release(t)
	endif
	set t = null
endfunction

function Buff_timerDestroyBuff takes nothing returns nothing
	call dispatch_Buff_destroyBuff(timer_getData(GetExpiredTimer()))
endfunction

		endif

endfunction

function CallbackCounted_callAndCount takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	call dispatch_CallbackCounted_call(this_42, this_42)
	set CallbackCounted_count[this_42] = CallbackCounted_count[this_42] + 1
	if CallbackCounted_count[this_42] >= CallbackCounted_maxCount[this_42] then
		call dispatch_CallbackCounted_destroyCallbackCounted(this_42)
	endif
endfunction

function dispatch_CallbackSingle_call takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	if CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling CallbackSingle.call")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called CallbackSingle.call on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	if CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 712 then
		if CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 702 then
			if CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 696 then
				if CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 662 then
					if CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 658 then
						call closure_impl_24(this_42)
					else
						call closure_impl_42(this_42)
					endif
				else
					call closure_impl_38(this_42)
				endif
			elseif CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 700 then
				if CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 698 then
					call closure_impl_27(this_42)
				else
					call closure_impl_26(this_42)
				endif
			else
				call closure_impl_39(this_42)
			endif
		elseif CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 708 then
			if CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 706 then
				if CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 704 then
					call closure_impl_28(this_42)
				else
					call closure_impl_30(this_42)
				endif
			else
				call closure_impl_23(this_42)
			endif
		elseif CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 710 then
			call closure_impl_43(this_42)
		else
			call closure_impl_41(this_42)
		endif
	elseif CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 724 then
		if CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 718 then
			if CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 716 then
				if CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 714 then
					call closure_impl_34(this_42)
				else
					call closure_impl_44(this_42)
				endif
			else
				call closure_impl_40(this_42)
			endif
		elseif CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 722 then
			if CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 720 then
				call closure_impl_36(this_42)
			else
				call closure_impl_25(this_42)
			endif
		else
			call closure_impl_33(this_42)
		endif
	elseif CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 730 then
		if CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 728 then
			if CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 726 then
				call closure_impl_35(this_42)
			else
				call closure_impl_32(this_42)
			endif
		else
			call closure_impl_29(this_42)
		endif
	elseif CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 732 then
		call closure_impl_37(this_42)
	else
		call closure_impl_31(this_42)
	endif
endfunction

function CallbackSingle_onDestroy takes integer this_42 returns nothing
endfunction

function dealloc_CallbackSingle takes integer obj returns nothing
	if CallbackSingle_typeId[obj] == 0 then
		call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Double free: object of type CallbackSingle")
		call I2S(1 / 0)
	else
		set CallbackSingle_nextFree[CallbackSingle_firstFree] = obj
		set CallbackSingle_firstFree = CallbackSingle_firstFree + 1
		set CallbackSingle_typeId[obj] = 0
	endif
endfunction

function destroyCallbackSingle takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	call CallbackSingle_onDestroy(this_42)
	call dealloc_CallbackSingle(this_42)
endfunction

		if CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 700 then
			if CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 662 then
				if CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 658 then
					if CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 651 then
						call destroyCallbackSingle(this_42)
					else
						call destroyCallbackSingle(this_42)
					endif
				else
					call destroyCallbackSingle(this_42)
				endif
			elseif CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 698 then
				if CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 696 then
					call destroyCallbackSingle(this_42)
				else
					call destroyCallbackSingle(this_42)
				endif
			else
				call destroyCallbackSingle(this_42)
			endif
		elseif CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 706 then
			if CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 704 then
				if CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 702 then
					call destroyCallbackSingle(this_42)
				else

			else

			endif
		elseif CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 710 then

			else

			endif

			if CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 720 then
				call destroyCallbackSingle(this_42)
			else
				call destroyCallbackSingle(this_42)
			endif
		else
			call destroyCallbackSingle(this_42)
		endif
	elseif CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 730 then
		if CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 728 then
			if CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 726 then
				call destroyCallbackSingle(this_42)
			else
				call destroyCallbackSingle(this_42)
			endif
		else
			call destroyCallbackSingle(this_42)
		endif
	elseif CallbackSingle_typeId[this_42] <= 732 then
		call destroyCallbackSingle(this_42)
	else
		call destroyCallbackSingle(this_42)
	endif
endfunction

function CallbackSingle_staticCallback takes nothing returns nothing
	local timer t = GetExpiredTimer()

function CustomBar_copyForce takes nothing returns nothing
	call ForceAddPlayer(CustomBar_tempForce, GetEnumPlayer())
endfunction

function CustomBar_unlock takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	if  not CustomBar_locked[this_42] then
		return
	endif
	set CustomBar_count = CustomBar_count - 1
	if CustomBar_count == 0 then
		call PauseTimer(CustomBar_animationTimer)
	endif
	set CustomBar_bars[CustomBar_lockindex[this_42]] = CustomBar_bars[CustomBar_count]
	set CustomBar_lockindex[CustomBar_bars[CustomBar_count]] = CustomBar_lockindex[this_42]
	set CustomBar_locked[this_42] = false
endfunction

function dispatch_CustomBar_unlock takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	if CustomBar_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling CustomBar.unlock")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called CustomBar.unlock on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	call CustomBar_unlock(this_42)
endfunction

function CustomBar_onDestroy takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	if CustomBar_t[this_42] != null then
		call DestroyTextTag(CustomBar_t[this_42])
	endif
	if CustomBar_locked[this_42] then
		call dispatch_CustomBar_unlock(this_42)
	endif
endfunction

function dealloc_CustomBar takes integer obj returns nothing
	if CustomBar_typeId[obj] == 0 then
		call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Double free: object of type CustomBar")
		call I2S(1 / 0)
	else
		set CustomBar_firstFree = CustomBar_firstFree + 1
		set CustomBar_typeId[obj] = 0
	endif
endfunction

function destroyCustomBar takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	call CustomBar_onDestroy(this_42)
	call dealloc_CustomBar(this_42)
endfunction

function dispatch_CustomBar_destroyCustomBar takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	if CustomBar_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling CustomBar.destroyCustomBar")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called CustomBar.destroyCustomBar on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	call destroyCustomBar(this_42)
endfunction

function CustomBar_fadeOutCallback takes nothing returns nothing
	local integer bar = timer_getData(GetExpiredTimer())
	set CustomBar_t[bar] = null
	call dispatch_CustomBar_destroyCustomBar(bar)
	call timer_release(GetExpiredTimer())
endfunction

function CustomBar_lockCallback takes nothing returns nothing
	local integer i = CustomBar_count - 1
	local integer s
	local integer tempIndex
	local integer tempIndex_2
	local integer tempIndex_3
	local real tempTupleSelectionResult_1
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_3
	local integer tempIndex_4
	local real tempTupleSelectionResult_2
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_3_2
	local integer tempIndex_5
	local real tempTupleSelectionResult_3
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_3
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_3
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_3_3
	local texttag temp
	local real temp_2
	local real temp_3
	loop
		exitwhen i < 0
		set s = CustomBar_bars[i]
		set tempIndex = s
		set CustomBar_position[tempIndex] = GetUnitX(CustomBar_u[s])
		set tempIndex_2 = s
		set CustomBar_position_2[tempIndex_2] = GetUnitY(CustomBar_u[s])
		set temp = CustomBar_t[s]
		set tempIndex_3 = s
		set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1 = CustomBar_position[tempIndex_3]
		set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2 = CustomBar_position_2[tempIndex_3]
		set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_3 = CustomBar_position_3[tempIndex_3]
		set tempTupleSelectionResult_1 = temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1
		set temp_2 = tempTupleSelectionResult_1 + CustomBar_xOffset[s]
		set tempIndex_4 = s
		set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2 = CustomBar_position[tempIndex_4]
		set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2 = CustomBar_position_2[tempIndex_4]
		set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_3_2 = CustomBar_position_3[tempIndex_4]
		set tempTupleSelectionResult_2 = temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2
		set temp_3 = tempTupleSelectionResult_2 + CustomBar_yOffset[s]
		set tempIndex_5 = s
		set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_3 = CustomBar_position[tempIndex_5]
		set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_3 = CustomBar_position_2[tempIndex_5]
		set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_3_3 = CustomBar_position_3[tempIndex_5]
		set tempTupleSelectionResult_3 = temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_3_3
		call SetTextTagPos(temp, temp_2, temp_3, tempTupleSelectionResult_3)
		set i = i - 1
	endloop
	set temp = null
endfunction

		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called Dot.getNext on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	set getNext_result = LinkedListModule_getNext(this_42)
	return getNext_result
endfunction

function Event_onDestroy takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	local integer buffer1 = Event_first[this_42]
	local integer buffer2
	loop
		exitwhen  not (buffer1 != 0)
		set buffer2 = Action_next[buffer1]
		call dispatch_Action_destroyAction(buffer1)
		set buffer1 = buffer2
	endloop
endfunction

endfunction

		call I2S(1 / 0)
	else
		set Event_nextFree[Event_firstFree] = obj
		set Event_firstFree = Event_firstFree + 1
		set Event_typeId[obj] = 0
	endif
endfunction

		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called Unit2Event.destroyUnit2Event on invalid object.")

		endif
	endif
	call destroyUnit2Event(this_42)
endfunction

function Shield_onDestroy takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	set ShieldList_shieldSum[Shield_referingList[this_42]] = ShieldList_shieldSum[Shield_referingList[this_42]] - Shield_amount[this_42]
	call timer_release(Shield_t[this_42])
	if Shield_shieldDestroyed[this_42] != 0 then
		call dispatch_Unit2Event_destroyUnit2Event(Shield_shieldDestroyed[this_42])
	endif
	if Shield_prev[this_42] != 0 then
		set Shield_next[Shield_prev[this_42]] = Shield_next[this_42]
	endif
	if Shield_next[this_42] != 0 then
		set Shield_prev[Shield_next[this_42]] = Shield_prev[this_42]
	endif
	if ShieldList_first[Shield_referingList[this_42]] == this_42 then
		set ShieldList_first[Shield_referingList[this_42]] = Shield_next[this_42]
	endif
	if ShieldList_last[Shield_referingList[this_42]] == this_42 then
		set ShieldList_last[Shield_referingList[this_42]] = Shield_prev[this_42]
	endif
endfunction

function dealloc_Shield takes integer obj returns nothing
	if Shield_typeId[obj] == 0 then
		call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Double free: object of type Shield")
		call I2S(1 / 0)
	else
		set Shield_nextFree[Shield_firstFree] = obj
		set Shield_firstFree = Shield_firstFree + 1
		set Shield_typeId[obj] = 0
	endif
endfunction

function destroyShield takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	call Shield_onDestroy(this_42)
	call dealloc_Shield(this_42)
endfunction

function dispatch_Shield_destroyShield takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	if Shield_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling Shield.destroyShield")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called Shield.destroyShield on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	call destroyShield(this_42)
endfunction

function ShieldList_damage takes integer this_42, real amount_39, integer source returns real
	local real remainingDmg
	local integer pos
	local integer buffer
	if ShieldList_first[this_42] == 0 then
		return amount_39
	endif
	if amount_39 > ShieldList_shieldSum[this_42] then
		set ShieldList_shieldSum[this_42] = 0.
	else
		set ShieldList_shieldSum[this_42] = ShieldList_shieldSum[this_42] - amount_39
	endif
	set remainingDmg = amount_39
	set pos = ShieldList_first[this_42]
	loop
		exitwhen  not (remainingDmg > 0. and pos != 0)
		if Shield_amount[pos] >= remainingDmg then
			set Shield_amount[pos] = Shield_amount[pos] - remainingDmg
			return 0.
		else
			set remainingDmg = remainingDmg - Shield_amount[pos]
			set Shield_amount[pos] = 0.
			if Shield_shieldDestroyed[pos] != 0 then
				call dispatch_Unit2Event_fire(Shield_shieldDestroyed[pos], source, Shield_target[pos])
			endif
			set buffer = pos
			set pos = Shield_next[buffer]
			call dispatch_Shield_destroyShield(buffer)
		endif
	endloop
	return remainingDmg
endfunction

function dispatch_ShieldList_damage takes integer this_42, real amount_39, integer source returns real
	local real damage_result
	if ShieldList_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling ShieldList.damage")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called ShieldList.damage on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	set damage_result = ShieldList_damage(this_42, amount_39, source)
	return damage_result
endfunction

function unit_kill takes unit this_42 returns nothing
	call KillUnit(this_42)
endfunction

function Unit_kill takes integer this_42, integer source returns nothing
	local integer i
	local integer goldAmount
	if  not Unit_isDead[this_42] then
		set Unit_isDead[this_42] = true
		call unit_addAbility(Unit_u[this_42], 1684365668)
		if Unit_onDeath[this_42] != 0 then
			call dispatch_Unit2Event_fire(Unit_onDeath[this_42], source, this_42)
		endif
		if Unit_causeDeath[this_42] != 0 then
			call dispatch_Unit2Event_fire(Unit_causeDeath[this_42], source, this_42)
		endif
		set i = 0
		loop
			exitwhen i > 11
			if dispatch_Table_loadReal(Unit_playerDamage[this_42], i) != 0. then
				set goldAmount = roundReal(dispatch_Table_loadReal(Unit_playerDamage[this_42], i) / Unit_totalDamage[this_42] * Unit_bounty[this_42])
				call SetPlayerState(Player(i), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD, GetPlayerState(Player(i), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD) + goldAmount)
				call dispatch_Unit_goldTT(this_42, goldAmount * 1., Player(i))
			endif
			set i = i + 1
		endloop
		call unit_kill(Unit_u[this_42])
	endif
endfunction

function Unit_dealDamage takes integer this_42, real amount_39, integer source, boolean reward returns boolean
	local real tHP
	local real currentAmount
	if Unit_isHero[source] then
	endif
	if Unit_vunerable[this_42] then
		set tHP = unit_getHP(Unit_u[this_42])
		set currentAmount = dispatch_ShieldList_damage(Unit_shieldList[this_42], amount_39, source)
		set Unit_totalDamage[this_42] = Unit_totalDamage[this_42] + amount_39
		if  not reward then
			set Unit_systemDamage[this_42] = Unit_systemDamage[this_42] + amount_39
		endif
		if tHP - 0.405 <= currentAmount then
			if reward then
				call dispatch_Table_saveReal(Unit_playerDamage[this_42], Unit_ownerId[this_42], dispatch_Table_loadReal(Unit_playerDamage[this_42], Unit_ownerId[this_42]) + tHP)
			endif
			call dispatch_Unit_kill(this_42, source)
		elseif reward then
			call dispatch_Table_saveReal(Unit_playerDamage[this_42], Unit_ownerId[this_42], dispatch_Table_loadReal(Unit_playerDamage[this_42], Unit_ownerId[this_42]) + amount_39)
		endif
		call unit_setHP(Unit_u[this_42], tHP - currentAmount)
		if Unit_isHero[this_42] or Unit_isHero[source] then
			return true
		else
			return false
		endif
	else
		if Unit_isHero[this_42] or Unit_isHero[source] then
			call dispatch_Unit_invuTT(this_42)
		endif
		return false
	endif
endfunction

function Hero_dealDamage takes integer this_42, real amount_39, integer source, boolean bonus returns boolean
	call dispatch_Bar_update(Hero_hb[this_42])
	return Unit_dealDamage(this_42, amount_39, source, bonus)
endfunction

function dispatch_Unit_dealDamage takes integer this_42, real amount_39, integer source, boolean reward returns boolean
	local boolean dealDamage_result
	if Unit_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling Unit.dealDamage")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called Unit.dealDamage on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	if Unit_typeId[this_42] <= 693 then
		set dealDamage_result = Unit_dealDamage(this_42, amount_39, source, reward)
	else
		set dealDamage_result = Hero_dealDamage(this_42, amount_39, source, reward)
	endif
	return dealDamage_result
endfunction

	set mbi = multiboard_getItem(InstanceBoard_mb, ShowInstances_classId_2, 1)
	set receiver = mbi
	call multiboarditem_setValue(receiver, int_toString(InstanceBoard_count[ShowInstances_classId_2]))

	set mbi = null
	set receiver = null
endfunction

function AttackOrder_issueToUnit takes integer this_42, unit u_2 returns boolean
	call trigger_disable(GetOrders_orderDetect)
	call IssueTargetOrderById(u_2, AttackOrder_atkOrderId, AttackOrder_target[this_42])
	call trigger_enable(GetOrders_orderDetect)
	return GetUnitAbilityLevel(u_2, 1684365668) == 1
endfunction

function MoveOrder_issueToUnit takes integer this_42, unit u_2 returns boolean
	local real currentPos_x
	local real currentPos_y
	local boolean b
	local integer tempIndex
	local real tempTupleSelectionResult_1
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2
	local integer tempIndex_2
	local real tempTupleSelectionResult_2
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2
	local real temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2
	local real temp_currentPos_x
	local real temp_currentPos_y
	local integer tempIndex_3
	local integer tempIndex_4
	local unit temp
	local integer temp_2
	local real temp_3
	local real temp_4
	call trigger_disable(GetOrders_orderDetect)
	set temp = u_2
	set temp_2 = MoveOrder_moveOrderId
	set tempIndex = this_42
	set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1 = MoveOrder_pos[tempIndex]
	set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2 = MoveOrder_pos_2[tempIndex]
	set tempTupleSelectionResult_1 = temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1
	set temp_3 = tempTupleSelectionResult_1
	set tempIndex_2 = this_42
	set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_1_2 = MoveOrder_pos[tempIndex_2]
	set temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2 = MoveOrder_pos_2[tempIndex_2]
	set tempTupleSelectionResult_2 = temp_tempTupleSelectionResult_2_2
	call IssuePointOrderById(temp, temp_2, temp_3, tempTupleSelectionResult_2)
	call trigger_enable(GetOrders_orderDetect)
	set temp_currentPos_x = unit_getPos(u_2)
	set temp_currentPos_y = unit_getPos_return_y
	set currentPos_x = temp_currentPos_x
	set currentPos_y = temp_currentPos_y
	set temp_4 = currentPos_x
	set tempIndex_3 = this_42
	set b = temp_4 == MoveOrder_lastPos[tempIndex_3] and currentPos_y == MoveOrder_lastPos_2[tempIndex_3]
	set tempIndex_4 = this_42
	set MoveOrder_lastPos[tempIndex_4] = currentPos_x
	set MoveOrder_lastPos_2[tempIndex_4] = currentPos_y
	set temp = null
	return b
endfunction

function dispatch_Order_issueToUnit takes integer this_42, unit u_2 returns boolean
	local boolean issueToUnit_result
	if Order_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling Order.issueToUnit")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called Order.issueToUnit on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	if Order_typeId[this_42] <= 683 then
		set issueToUnit_result = MoveOrder_issueToUnit(this_42, u_2)
	else
		set issueToUnit_result = AttackOrder_issueToUnit(this_42, u_2)
	endif
	return issueToUnit_result
endfunction

		set this_42 = SEntry_nextFree[SEntry_firstFree]
	endif
	return this_42

	set SEntry_elem[this_42] = elem
	set SEntry_next[this_42] = next
endfunction

	call construct_SEntry_2(this_42, elem, next)
	return this_42
endfunction

function Queue_enqueue takes integer this_42, integer elem returns nothing
	if Queue_front[this_42] == Queue_dummy[this_42] then
		set Queue_front[this_42] = new_SEntry_2(elem, Queue_dummy[this_42])
		set Queue_back[this_42] = Queue_front[this_42]
	else
		set SEntry_next[Queue_back[this_42]] = new_SEntry_2(elem, Queue_dummy[this_42])
		set Queue_back[this_42] = SEntry_next[Queue_back[this_42]]
	endif
	set Queue_size[this_42] = Queue_size[this_42] + 1
endfunction

function dispatch_Queue_enqueue takes integer this_42, integer elem returns nothing
	if Queue_typeId[this_42] == 0 then
		if this_42 == 0 then
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Nullpointer exception when calling Queue.enqueue")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		else
			call BJDebugMsg("|cffFF3A29Wurst Error:|r" + "Called Queue.enqueue on invalid object.")
			call I2S(1 / 0)
		endif
	endif
	call Queue_enqueue(this_42, elem)
endfunction

function construct_Order takes integer this_42 returns nothing
	local multiboarditem mbi
	local multiboarditem receiver
	set InstanceBoard_count[ShowInstances_classId_2] = InstanceBoard_count[ShowInstances_classId_2] + 1
	set mbi = multiboard_getItem(InstanceBoard_mb, ShowInstances_classId_2, 1)
	set receiver = mbi
	call multiboarditem_setValue(receiver, int_toString(InstanceBoard_count[ShowInstances_classId_2]))
	call multiboarditem_release(receiver)
	set mbi = null
	set receiver = null
endfunction
